Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Speeches  
35  
Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Speech Compilation Committee  

Foreword  
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
What Kind of Life Will I Leave Behind?  
<Prayer> Today is September 27, 1970. On this last Sabbath of the month, we, the children gathered here this morning and those scattered across the nation, bow down before you, so please look upon us with compassion.  
As we stand before you this morning, may we pledge and resolve to become a victorious offering before you, in order to take responsibility for the reality we face, in light of the hard work you have endured throughout the historical ages.  
As we reflect on the countless ancestors who have borne the cross before you and lived their lives as objects of sorrow, we realize that we, in this era, must repay our debts before you and leave something behind for you.  
Father, please examine the foundation of our hearts. Help us to reflect on whether we have become individuals who possess a heart that can truly welcome your presence.  
When you come among us, who will you visit first, and who among us will receive your attention as we look to you and move? In aligning our hearts with yours, no human can be the motive; it has always been you who have been the motive at any time.  
On September 27, 1970, at the Headquarters Church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
* Here, the title is based on the main theme of the speech, and it is noted that the titles differ in the English edition as 'what we should do in our lifetime,' in the Japanese edition as '生涯において何をなすづきか,' and in the Korean edition as '생애에 무엇을 남길 것인가.'  
8   What Kind of Life Will I Leave Behind?  
When we think about the position we must take, realizing that you must always look upon us and come to us, we feel that you are indeed a pitiful Father.  
Before humanity has experienced the many sorrows of history, you have suffered first, and we realize that this is a debt we can never repay. We reflect on how long it has been since we have known that such a Father exists, and we also consider how many times we have failed to recognize this. When we think about the one-sided nature of your historical providence in seeking out such unworthy children, we come to understand that you, our Father, have been pitiful not only in our time but throughout generations and even for our descendants.  
We must understand that you are a lonely Father, a sorrowful Father, and one who endures hardships. We must come to know this.  
When one faces difficulties, if there are sons and daughters who can worry about how you, our Father, would feel, then we must realize that you look upon them with pride and joy as they share in the heavenly victory.  
Even if one’s life is at its last moment, they must become sons and daughters who can hold the heart that you have gone through such places and endured such things. If there are sons and daughters who comfort you before worrying about themselves and walk the final path of life, then you hold a heartfelt desire for those sons and daughters to unite with you in a way that no one else can.  
As we think of the many ancestors who have come and gone on the path of restoration, from Abel of Adam's family to Noah, Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, and through Moses and John the Baptist to the countless prophets after Jesus, we must consider how much sorrow has accumulated and how many of your sighs have been left behind during those times of bloodshed. If all of this sorrow and sighing were to remain only with you, it would be one thing, but the circumstances of your sorrow cannot be so, and we realize that your sorrow remains before our lives.  
9  
Here, gathered are your children, some at 60 years old, some at 40, some as young men, and some as boys, all struggling to weave new lives by following your path, so please look upon these children with compassion. Rather than protecting us from any environment of the cross, please allow us to overcome that cross, and rather than shielding us from loneliness, may we become sons and daughters who can overcome that loneliness.  
When we look at the current reality of the Republic of Korea before us, who will take responsibility for this nation? We cannot help but think of this unbelievable reality where it seems no one can take responsibility. In this current environment, we cannot hope to rely on anyone to bless this nation and this people.  
Father, yet we know that you cannot abandon this nation and this people. If there are sons and daughters who are concerned about the future of this nation and people, holding a heartfelt desire to serve you, we must understand that you are a Father who wishes to relate to those sons and daughters with a heart full of gratitude.  
The people who can serve the world and be honored in the world are not those who claim to be great. We must truly understand that it is you, who does not reveal yourself and endures the path of hardship in solitude, who can do so. We need sons and daughters who, rather than taking joy for themselves, strive to turn that joy back to you, thinking of you and working silently.  
O hardworking Father, O lonely Father, you have endured extreme sorrow by closing your eyes, biting your lips, and holding back your tongue, and we must feel that we are truly your sons and daughters who understand your circumstances.  
We must realize that you cannot be comforted by those who seek satisfaction in their daily lives, while you bear the grief of a millennium.  
10   What Kind of Life Will I Leave Behind?  
Before such a Father, we must have a humble and gentle attitude, and while living a true life, even if we must live with tears, we must lead a life of reverence, a life of awakening, as we pass through the historical ages. However, we must realize that we have instead troubled you, placed heavier burdens of the cross upon you, and driven you into a lonely path. We must also recognize that we stood in the forefront of striking those on the side of heaven as descendants who inherited a wicked lineage.  
Thus, we must discover that we cannot seek forgiveness before you with anything in the universe.  
Therefore, we must have the heart to offer our lives, which have caused you to sigh and grieve before your will, in order to truly seek you and face you. We must realize that this is the most significant matter in our lives, and we earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Father, our Unification Church is in a lonely position. When we realize that the bloodline of countless ancestors who came out according to the bond of unification is to be connected through this altar today, we understand that this place, where the blood of our ancestors is intertwined, is a solemn, serious, and sacred place.  
When we feel once again how foolish and weightless we have been before you today, we must have the heart to bow our faces down, shedding tears and sweat before you, and repent, realizing that we cannot hide our sinful appearances.  
Yet, we forget such appearances and become proud, longing only for our own happiness. We must realize this, Father, and earnestly hope and wish for it.  
The sons and daughters who bow down here must forget their own existence and become those who can entrust everything to you and discuss it with a holy heart. We reflect once more on your life, which seeks out the pitiful multitude and befriends the lonely.  
As we think of your sorrowful figure, who awakens your children through the historical process, we must realize that we must not only desire to become your sons and daughters but also recognize that we have already become your sons and daughters, and we must look upon your figure with that conviction.  
In a place where sorrow reaches its peak, and tears cloud our vision, is there no son who can embrace the teacher who has lost direction and advise him to walk this path? Is there no daughter who can do the same? Therefore, we must understand that you are a pitiful Father.  
As we regret the past, how many of us are here who can take our sinful appearances and lead the lonely hand of our Father, who has left a history of sorrow, over the rugged mountain peaks, promising to take responsibility?  
Father, we must become sons and daughters who can recall the past, criticize the present, and face the future while calling upon you.  
When we realize that there is no way to comfort the lonely Father with anything, and that we cannot comfort the sorrowful and troubled Father with anything, we must learn to shed tears of lamentation, and even if the horror and loneliness make us forget ourselves, we must remain as sons and daughters whom you can remember until the moment our lives end. If there are such sons and daughters, then you will seek me out, and we must become sons and daughters who cherish the fact that we are connected to you more than anything else in our lives.  
Father, the sorrowful 1960s have passed. Now, as we enter the 1970s, we must become true filial children. We must be certain that being a mere verbal filial child will not allow us to present ourselves.  
When we reflect on our past, we discover that we are so ashamed that regret clouds our vision and we can hardly move. We must become sons and daughters who are distressed that we, who should walk before you, have instead followed behind you, struggling to take the path you walked. If we become such sons and daughters, we will greet a bright future, and our future will develop alongside your desires.  
Therefore, we must not be careless and boastful before you, claiming to be your representatives. Please allow us to be sons and daughters who can serve only you and follow only you. We admire the deep, wide, high, holy, and dignified image of you in our hearts. We pursue the glorious and dignified image of you rather than the shabby, sorrowful, and lonely Father.  
To achieve this, we must understand that you alone cannot solve this. We must realize that your sons and daughters must create the foundation and platform for this to happen. Thus, we must become your sons and daughters who can straighten your path, value your living environment, and work harder to return glorious glory before the path of your victory.  
As we put forth all our effort, we must forget that we might perish and be consumed ourselves, and instead, we must become sons and daughters who can rejoice in seeing you grow, be happy, and be praised. We earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Father, come to this place. Come to this place with a heart of hope. Bring us a new light of hope. May your hope always be in our hearts, so that we may be drawn closer to you, and may we have a heart of admiration that can uplift you, realizing that we are your sons and daughters and recognizing that we are your representatives.  
If we cannot do this, then please look upon us with your fiery eyes, so that we may be freed from the hands of sin and that only the bonds and foundations of our true nature can be absorbed and integrated to unite with you, Father.  
13  
Father, please protect the future path of our thirty million people. You know the tragic history of this nation, which has woven a sorrowful history of bloodshed due to the division between North and South Korea. The love for this nation must be higher and deeper than the thirty-eighth parallel. We must have a mindset that considers North Korea as our own hands and feet.  
When we think that the Unification Church is the only group that can take responsibility for this nation, we must become a group that holds onto the sorrow of this people and strives to overcome it.  
As we worry about the fate of the thirty million people in the future, we have set a period of sincerity to offer our devotion, so please protect this nation. This nation and people must not trust anyone but you. We must stand close to you. More than anyone, we must strive to become a group of unification that can do so.  
Father, please protect this pitiful nation. Have compassion on this people who have left a history of sorrow before you as you seek hope. We know that wrongdoing is always a bait in human life.
We beseech you to forgive the wrongdoings of this nation. Now, we must become a group that can prepare the way for your coming. Even if we are looked down upon by others, let this nation be one that repents the past with tears and seeks to unite before you anew in this present age. Since we have not yet become such a nation, we must deeply realize that the mission of the Unification Church remains to make this nation into one.

Centered around the Unification Church, at the moment we cross the final path of death, what will we leave behind before the Father? When we gather our sons and daughters, or our disciples who follow us, or what we will leave for our colleagues and the nation, let us be able to say, "I am a son who has left such and such," or "I am a daughter who has left such and such." Father, we are not those who blindly follow the circumstances of this age; we are a group that must lead this era and establish a new history, so we earnestly hope and wish that you remember us.

We acknowledge that the footprints we have walked so far and the appearances we have fought with have been extremely inadequate. We understand that we must gather our weary bodies and minds and present ourselves before you as polished stones. Yet, if we find ourselves in a position where we cannot even muster the strength of one body, Father, we earnestly ask that you take responsibility and help us regain our strength.

We have a mission to create a victorious unification front before you in this 1970s, so we have carried the banner of unification through individuals, nations, and the world. We recognize that our mission, which must be left through the WACL conference centered on Japan, depends on that nation.

Let us cross the barriers of Asia and the world, and even after they return to their countries, may they establish bonds that they cannot forget, filled with true and earnest hearts that long for each other. To hasten the day when the enemies scattered across the world surrender, may we become a path that can bind all our efforts together, and may their hearts remain as a foundation of victory before their nations.

When we think of how the Father has driven and beaten the little children, we feel infinitely sorry for them, but we realize that the Father, who must command them to go again and again, is even more pitiable. We come to understand how much lonelier the gap between heaven and the world is than the lonely gaps between nations. We earnestly hope and wish that your comfort and compassion may be with those who cannot help but urge them to run again.

During this time, we have moved forward, building our sincerity while facing much criticism. Some have even appealed to you with a heavy heart while being criticized on the streets. We are grateful that you have taken care of all these circumstances and brought victory before us. This victory must become a condition that we can proudly boast of through this nation.

We do not wish for this nation to stand in a position cursed before you, so we earnestly hope and wish that you help us understand how significant a responsibility the Unification Church bears in the future.

Korea, Japan, and China, which must take responsibility for tomorrow's Asia, must not only suggest a direction to prepare a foundation to fight against communism in cooperation with the imperial nations of Asia but also cultivate the strength to establish a society of coexistence and justice.

Father, we deeply feel that when something happens, there is lamentation for those who are unprepared. We know that a nation that does not strive will be invaded and lose its freedom. The more we feel that our hearts are like this, the more we must strive. We must work day and night. Even when others are asleep, we must save our sleeping time to prepare. While others walk their own paths and leave their own lives, we must save and invest all our efforts for the nation and the world. We earnestly ask that the Unification Church fulfill this mission.

Father, please protect this morning. In just a few days, October will come. In October, there is a historic event centered around 777 couples that has never occurred in the historical age, so if there are your sons and daughters who are staying up all night with sincerity for this matter, please take care of them a thousandfold. Comfort them with a heart of love and guide them with a hand of grace. We earnestly ask and wish that you gather everything according to your providence.

Father, today, according to the promise you have allowed, I will visit this earth, so please be with us here. Comfort their hearts that long for the headquarters, and comfort their hearts that wish to meet the teacher. They should not meet anyone in the world with that feeling. May today’s meeting be an opportunity to feel your circumstances and to leave a new victory in the 1970s.

When I think of the children scattered across foreign lands who admire Korea as the homeland of faith, I must feel how heavy the responsibility of this Cheongpyeong headquarters is. We must not become a shameful figure before those who live before you, shedding tears and appealing to you while staying up all night. We must realize that we should not become members of the headquarters who are advised by them, asking, "What are you doing while we are doing this?"

Let your sons and daughters gathered here struggle to leave a life that can remain before your will, centering on you while saving time. Let them be sons and daughters who struggle to go in place of your life.

May this year be blessed under your protection. The coming year of 1971 must be one we take on ourselves. After the day of blessing has passed, we are in a position where we must make a new start nationwide. Moreover, there is a period remaining where we must hasten the way for your sons and daughters, so Father, we earnestly ask that you guide us directly.

May everything go smoothly, and may we become a group that can pledge victory through this morning. I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> As you all know, today is the last Sunday of this month. This September has been a period of sincerity for our Unification Church, for our Korea, and even for Japan, centered around the unforgettable WACL conference.

Unification Church members who must take responsibility for this nation

The day we looked forward to with sincerity has already passed. We must give thanks to God for successfully concluding the WACL conference. In the future, we must realize that we need to think about our mission from a new perspective and be more sincere. Moreover, considering that the situation in Asia is rapidly changing and remains tense, we come to understand that we have a responsibility to be sincere for this nation and this people.

How can we look forward to the unification of North and South Korea in the 1970s? When will the day of resolution that this nation desires be achieved? This is a significant cross that must be borne by the nation. The issue of unification in Korea is not just a matter for the Korean people; it is a problem that affects Asia and is connected to the world.

The primary responsibility for this does not lie with any world or Asia but must be borne by our Han people. If the people of South Korea are in a position to bear this responsibility, then specifically, who will take on that responsibility? Ordinary members of society cannot bear it. The religious organizations that have a spiritual influence on society must take on that responsibility. Or, some religion that has shared a historical bond up to now must take responsibility for this reality. It is an undeniable fact that those who have a spiritual attitude must take responsibility for the path of this nation.

So, when we consider which organization will take on that responsibility, it seems that not only we but also the general public believes that it must be the Unification Church. From that perspective, our spiritual attitude and our way of life become issues.

We must have a loyalty to our nation that is not just loyalty. The motivation for the realization of myriad matters must be formed around us. In this light, we must consider whether we have truly become those who can do so.

From this standpoint, the beginning and outcome of fulfilling the responsibilities our organization bears ultimately depend on each individual member of the Unification Church. The issue is about me. You yourselves are the issue. Even if I am a small individual, the conclusion is that whether or not I can spark the spirit of the nation tomorrow depends on me.

When we must renew our awareness and commitment to our responsibilities toward the nation

In that sense, the question of what kind of life I will leave behind becomes significant. Looking at your lives today, some may be close to 60 years old, some may be over 40, and some may be very young.

In this context, what kind of life will you leave behind? You must have a heart that worries about the path of this nation and feel the mission you must undertake. Older individuals may realize that they have no achievements in their past lives when they reflect on their past, and they may feel that no matter how hard they try and struggle, they cannot reach the limits they envision. However, the more they understand and feel this, the more they must not despair but instead resolve to invest all their energy into their remaining short lives to bring about the final resolution.

They should not worry just because they are older; they must concentrate all their remaining lives and make a new commitment regarding how they will invest that in front of the nation and history. The same goes for the youth. If there are young people in their 20s who embrace their hopeful hearts and have a new hope to take responsibility for the future of this nation, that hope is good. 

But how can that hope be realized? How can they assert themselves and achieve their desires while navigating their surroundings? They must think about how to lead that environment, influence it, comfort the lonely, empower the weak, instill hope for tomorrow in them, and consider how to spend their remaining lives. This is not something to be taken lightly.

We must carry the weight of the connections that extend in all directions, and we must pursue a meaningful life while sympathizing with many who are sad, lonely, in difficulty, or suffering. No matter how much a young person boasts of their youth and dreams of tomorrow, they must understand that such dreams may be achieved for their own sake but cannot stand in a position of responsibility for the nation or this era.

From this perspective, whether young or old, we in the Unification Church must realize that we have received a heavenly mission and must stand in a position to strive for the purpose we have been called to achieve. Therefore, the question of how we should spend our lives today is a serious matter. Thus, you must become the resurrection of history.

As citizens of the Republic of Korea, looking at our ancestors who have come and gone throughout history, there would have been no ancestor who did not wish for this nation, the Republic of Korea, to become a strong nation rather than a weak one in Asia. However, at one point, they could not appear on this land to fulfill that hope, which has now been realized.

When we think about this fact, the question becomes whether we can become a hopeful reality that can fulfill the historical desires that our ancestors have worried about. 

To the 30 million people of our nation, we must instill the understanding that Korea must be this and that, and that we must undertake a new historical mission centered around economic revival in the Asia-Pacific era. We must become the subjectivity that can stimulate the people of this nation to instill tomorrow's new hope and encourage them to renew their hearts.

In that sense, the question is whether you have become those who can replace the subjectivity of reality before this nation. 

We cannot walk a smooth path.

Even if we have been in such a position historically and presently, when we consider where there is a group that can give hope to the nation for the future or an individual who can give hope to individuals, we must be recognized by this nation as "they must be the ones. They must be these people."

From that position, when you look at the 38th parallel, that 38th parallel is not the 38th parallel of the Republic of Korea; it is the 38th parallel of our Unification Church.

Through the small group of unification, we must reclaim the land of North Korea, where more than 13 million people live. We have been entrusted with the responsibility and mission to seek a way to reclaim that place. Regardless of the cost of sacrifice, even if no one is left, we must mobilize everyone to carry out this task.

From this perspective, when we look at the 38th parallel, we must ask what kind of operation we should conduct. Should we conduct a normal operation? We must be able to boldly declare our ideology and background, saying, "We have this ideology and this background; if you want to challenge us, then challenge us."
what kind of life will I leave behind? 

So what kind of operation will we undertake? If there is only one method to achieve our purpose, it is a surprise operation. There is no other option. When will we attempt this surprise operation? Will it be in broad daylight? No one attempts a surprise operation in broad daylight. It must be done at night. Not just any night, but a night when a fierce storm rages and torrential rain pours down. It must be a night that no one wants to face. 

Then, will the path be a highway? No. It will be a treacherous mountain path. It must be a deep mountain trail where no one has left footprints. Among the deep mountain paths, if there is the most difficult thorny path, that path will be one that can determine life or death. 

Who will take that path? It is not about going to the front lines and dying in battle. One must be a special forces unit that can naturally confront and overcome the environment that causes many casualties along the way. 

From this perspective, when we say that the Unification Church has taken on this mission in front of the Republic of Korea, there is no other path to fulfill that mission. Therefore, the question is what kind of mindset I should have here and how I should start. Without being prepared for death, one cannot march forward. Without the hope of being resurrected after death, one cannot bear this strategic mission. 

Thus, today, the members of the Unification Church must walk the path of suffering to fulfill that responsibility. They must become pioneers who overcome difficulties from a position that no one cares about, a position that can be said to be already dead, and pave the way for tomorrow's hope. This journey of life must continue for a year or even ten years, and even if it means dying along the way, it must be undertaken. If I cannot fulfill this responsibility, I must vow to guide my descendants to walk this path and teach them. Without doing this, we will perish. 

If I find myself in a desperate situation where I cannot escape this environment until my life is over, I must hold the hands of my comrades, my sons and daughters, and leave behind a will or advice for a hopeful tomorrow. Reflecting on my life so far, I must establish successors who can run further. 

From this perspective, if the Unification Church has taken on such a mission today, what kind of life will I leave behind? The Unification Church must not walk the smooth path that ordinary people have walked until now. We must not proceed with the resolve that ordinary people can recognize us as an ordinary church. We must take the path that is so abnormal that it cannot even be imagined, and we must be recognized as a church that can only be accepted as a miracle to have any hope of victory tomorrow. 

When considering this issue, we must recognize that we are in a new field today, and we must renew our resolve and critically reflect on ourselves. This is what the Unification Church must be today. 

What should the leaders of the Unification Church do? The same applies to all of you who follow the Unification Church. The more people there are, the more they must converge on a single focus and move forward. We were born to achieve that, we must live to complete and fulfill that, and we must die for that purpose. We must devote all our efforts to this goal, and we must invest all our energy to achieve it. All the equipment necessary for the fight must be prepared for this purpose, and you must understand that this is where it all leads. 

If the Unification Church fails to fulfill that responsibility, it will perish. The Unification Church will collapse. When pushing you toward the ultimate goal, you must be driven to the very limits. Many sacrifices will follow. If everyone collapses and only one person remains, what will happen then? This is the issue. 

When we look at that last remaining person, that person must truly be the embodiment of our hopes. If you find yourself in a position where you must uphold your responsibility and mission, risking your life to fulfill your heavenly mandate, what will you do? Will you retreat in battle? That cannot be the case. History is always changing. Because history is always changing, if an individual is sacrificed in that historical process, a day will surely come when they can be reborn along with that historical hope. 

Therefore, you must have an unwavering belief in that hope in your heart and invest all your sincerity into it. A wise person is one who dies with God, not with the enemy. Jesus lived such a life. Jesus tried with all his might to lead all of Israel, but everything fell apart. 

He wished to walk the path of destiny that he could not avoid, along with his disciples, but in the end, all his disciples abandoned him and fled. Not everyone died for the country; they went their own way, seeking their own desires. Only Jesus was the one who had to lay down his life to walk the path that could not be avoided. When we think about this, with whom did Jesus walk the path of the cross? 

The sincerity of Jesus, who could not walk with humanity, was stronger than that of anyone who followed God. Therefore, he felt a greater responsibility than anyone who had worked hard throughout history, and he had a stronger sense of purpose than anyone centered on that purpose. Jesus did not walk the path of the cross alone. He walked with God. 

Only that path could root a new tradition in the world of death and the world of enemies. We can feel this through the process of Jesus' final destiny being determined. When Jesus said, "Abba, Father, all things are possible for you; remove this cup from me. Yet not what I will, but what you will" (Mark 14:36), all the content is included in that. 

"I am now going to the Father. I do not go in a cowardly manner, but let me go according to your will. Many people who have come this far have not been able to go in the way you desire, but please let me go in the way you desire. As I go, let me leave behind a point of agreement that can align with the standard of being the son you wish for in this historical age." 

Even in such a lonely position, Jesus was always dignified. When he prayed, "Father, forgive them their sins," it was not the prayer of a loser. He returned to God, but he believed that the time would surely come when he would conquer the world. Even when that time of victory came, he did not treat this world as an enemy but instilled a worldview that could accept enemies. 

Although his own self, filled with such hope, would die and retreat, he blessed the Roman villains who would suffer defeat in the future, and the opposing groups, thereby becoming the motivation for conquering them inside and out. 

What will I leave behind in my life? 

Such a life of Jesus is worthy of respect before God and in the context of all historical traditions, including the history of forgiveness. In other words, Jesus lived a life that was not caught up in any external or internal issues. Therefore, Jesus' life did not end with those thirty years but remains a historical life to this day. 

Thus, the history up to now has developed to achieve the purpose that Jesus left behind. God has also been guiding history to fulfill that purpose, so for the direction to align with the goal, Christianity must become a global religion. Therefore, no matter what kind of persecution Christianity has gone through, it has not ended in failure; rather, as the fate of failure approaches, it has become a foundation for victory and has developed into a new global foundation. 

Today, the path of the Unification Church is the same. I must have the mindset that I was born for God and the world. In other words, I must have the belief that I was born to resolve the life-and-death issues of the world. We must cross the 38th parallel. Even if there is a greater 38th parallel, we must cross it. What we need to consider is that the issue is not the 38th parallel of the Korean people. What will happen when we break this and form a unified nation? There remains the 38th parallel with China and the Soviet Union that borders us. 

Today, the 38th parallel that divides North and South Korea is not such a great trial. While this is the 38th parallel centered on our people, we must also overcome the stronger and more extreme 38th parallel with the Soviet Union and China. To lay the groundwork for peace that our nation must resolve, we must establish a victorious foundation that can also overcome the greater 38th parallel. 

From this perspective, the 38th parallel of our country is not an issue. If our Korean people can resolve our 38th parallel and become a nation that can overcome the global 38th parallel bordering the Soviet Union and China, then this nation will undoubtedly instill a new subjectivity in the world and present a new direction. Do you truly have that belief? 

Even if the communist forces have established a global foothold and launch an attack against us, the question is whether we have become individuals and organizations that can confidently confront them without being overwhelmed and achieve victory. God has been seeking such organizations and individuals until now. 

The Communist Party has carried out its policies through deceptive tactics until now. This will eventually be condemned. Evil has not developed through a normal activity system. When we consider that it has invaded based on concealment and deceptive tactics, we can understand that this is the game centered around Satan's evil. This is the issue.

The Order of Good and Evil's Origin

Did good come first, or did evil come first? It is said that evil came first.

Evil that started from illicit love

So how did evil begin? It did not start from any external material conditions, but rather centered around the issue of love. The inevitable bloodline connection that arose from illicit love became the motive for the emergence of evil, which is the sorrow of humanity, and we must understand that this became the historical point of good and evil.

Each individual is born receiving the bloodline of their parents. You have been formed today through your parents' bloodline, originating from their love. No one can separate that nature which resembles their parents and acquire a different nature. From the perspective of the principle of creation, this is impossible.

Since the root of evil is also based on the nature of the parents, it is not easy to remove this root. If one is not careful, it can lead to the denial of the principle of creation. The root of sin is fundamentally tied to the bloodline.

God has been working for 6,000 years because this bloodline issue has been the motive. 

So how can this be corrected? Since falsehood and evil are opposed to good, one cannot enter the realm of good without being of the same lineage, direction, or purpose. In pursuing the world of good and the character of good, one cannot seek a new world of good with the historical direction and social systems that have been established until now.

So what must be done? The direction must be fundamentally changed. If one goes east, another must go west; if one goes south, another must go north; if one goes down, another must go up; if one goes up, another must go down. This is the origin of the contradictions that humanity has not been able to resolve until now.

If this is true, achieving hope through the heart of our nature that seeks good is not a simple matter. While it is the inherent desire of humanity to achieve this purpose, one cannot have a normal hope within an encircled environment. Regaining that hope is impossible without a revolutionary world.

The conclusion point of God's providence and human desire must be unified

What does religion seek and desire? Good. And who is the object that religion centers around? God. What the true person of God and true goodness aims for is to liberate humanity, which is in an environment of sin, and to make them into good value humans. This is our human wish and the providence of God through humanity.

The conclusion point of God's providence and human desire must be unified, and that point of unity is the point of completion. That completion is not achieved through external conditions. In this age of material civilization, where materialism is rampant, can the conclusion point of humanity's hope and the conclusion point of God's providence be determined based on material? That is utterly impossible.

Therefore, how can we manifest the true joy of a day of true love centered around true people and true God? The factors of life, hope, and happiness are to taste the joy of being reborn through love on a foundation where true people and true God can rejoice. There will be times when such joy appears in the history of humanity or in the value world pursued by humans. Since this is the standard that both humans and God hope for, we must take that standard as the decisive point of our wishes.

Thus, we must educate humanity within God's providence centered on that. In education, it is not only about teaching that to people but also about establishing a connection with it. This is the ultimate essence that God wants to spread through religion. When we examine the Bible of Christianity or the scriptures of various religions from this perspective, we can see that there is always such content.

A true person must love heaven. They must love the earth. They must love people. In other words, they must love heaven, earth, and humanity. One cannot love the earth first. Why? Because the earth is not the origin of love. One cannot love people first. Why? Because people are not the origin of love. So what is the origin of love? It is the absolute God. Therefore, a person who cannot love God cannot love people, and a person who cannot love people cannot love the earth and all things.

From this perspective, what is the highest standard of religion? It is to love God. Then comes loving people, and then comes loving all things. Your efforts to live simply and save resources centered around religion all stem from this. Therefore, we must have a foundation of love that respects humanity and aims for human equality.

This highest ideal, not only an external ideal for humanity but also the internal emotional issues that arise from the heart, must be protected and governed by the foundation of God, not oneself. God is the center. Therefore, a person who cannot love this center cannot love others in external fields.

If humans had received perfect love from God

Considering all of this, if God exists, what would be the first thing that God would teach humans? Would God have to love humans, or must humans love God? Which is the principle?

In the fallen world of humanity, it is the principle that God loves humans. What is the limit of that love? It is perfect love. We humans will demand perfect love. How wonderful it would have been if that perfect love had been given! If our lives had been determined on the foundation of perfect love, and if the external stage of life had unfolded through that love, how happy it would have been! When we think about this, we realize that we did not have the starting point to achieve that.

Therefore, it becomes a problem. If humans had received absolute love from the absolute God, what would have happened? How powerful would that love have been? It would have been the motive to develop vitality. Life must be governed by the power of that love. What is the most authoritative power that can influence our life and death issues? It is not the power of any external world. It is the power of love that arises from within. No one can deny that. Therefore, we often see life and death centered around love in our daily lives. This proves that love is stronger than life.

Did God completely love humanity within the realm of principled law? Also, when humans were originally created as sons and daughters, they were in a position to receive perfect love, but did humans receive that love? If they did, there would be no problem. The one who loved deeply can never be forgotten. The bond formed by such love cannot be severed by anyone, not even by parental advice or the teachings of a teacher.

If the absolute God and humanity had established a relationship of perfect love centered on the relationship of parent and child, how joyful and wonderful it would have been! If that had been the case, the history of humanity would not have been such a tragic history.

Love possesses the subjective power that encompasses all strength. Therefore, in the moment concentrated on love, one forgets everything and enters a realm where no other can interfere or establish a relationship. That is why people even commit suicide for love. When one is drawn into that, nothing external can interfere or relate to them. Being in such a position of concentrated subjective power is the essence of love. When we establish a relationship centered on the absolute power of God's love, nothing can invade that.

If our human ancestors had started from this origin, with God saying, "This is my beloved son and daughter," and standing in a position of eternal love, would humanity have become so miserable?

You do not know the existence of God. The question of whether God exists or not is a historical tragedy. If humanity and God had established a relationship of perfect love, the existence of God would be felt. Because of the love of God that transcends the consciousness of existence, the question of whether God exists or not would not matter. This itself is the sorrow of humanity being born into a different relationship due to the fall. You must keep this in mind.

From this standard, what should the numerous scriptures and those who walk the path of virtue teach us today? They must teach us about God's love. The goal of those on the path of virtue is to cultivate a character that can be completely united centered on God's love. Nothing else is necessary for humanity.

If one is born as a child, they must receive 100 percent of their parents' love. Otherwise, dissatisfaction arises. Isn’t that true for you? When you observe a parent loving their child, you cannot quantify that love. If a parent has a million units of love but only gives 900,000 to their child while keeping 100,000 for themselves, even if the child receives 900,000, they will feel as though they have not received love. Only when the remaining 100,000 is given will they feel that they have received all the love.

Later, when you marry and your spouse asks, "Do you love me?" you cannot say, "I love you 99 percent." You must say, "I love you 100 percent." Why? Because only love can establish a complete relationship, and only love can give and receive everything. To achieve unity, one must give everything and receive everything. That is how oneness is achieved. If unity is established here, it would be complete unity.

What kind of being is God to us?

So, who is God? God is the one who created me. If God created humans, how much care must have gone into that creation? Look closely at people. What if you were born without eyelashes? Have you thought about that? Eyelashes are there to prevent dust blown by the wind from entering the eyes. They act as barriers to block all incoming dust. Moreover, the eyes blink every day; who commanded that? Did you think to yourself, "I must blink my eyes"? Have you ever thought about that? The eyes blink every few seconds; who told them to do so? Can you say it was your father? If so, you would have to trace back to your father's parents, and so on, ultimately leading back to the absolute being. That is the one who created all of this.

Think about it. Did you think you had to be born with eyes like this, blinking, and with eyelashes? If you look closely, it seems absurd. But do you think these things just happened randomly, without thought, design, or planning? If there were no eyelashes, where would the rain go when it pours? All that rain would enter the eyes. The same goes for sweat. However, because the eyelashes act like mountain ranges, rain and sweat do not enter the eyes.

What if the eyeball were sunken? It is because the round eyeball is covered by eyelids that the rain flows around it. When we observe these things, we realize that there are scientific principles that our thoughts cannot fathom.
We can see the fact that it was created under a line. 
Also, take a look at the nose. Why is this nose attached here? If it just appeared on its own, it would be upside down. What would happen if it were upside down? Think about it. It would be quite nice on a rainy day. Why is it attached like this? It is not something that naturally came to be. 
That aside, what about the nose hairs? Why are they attached like this? If this is strange, then it is indeed strange; if it is unfortunate, then it is unfortunate; if it is bizarre, then it is truly bizarre. Now, take a look at the hands. What would happen if the hands were reversed? That wouldn’t work. What if there was only one hand? Everything is designed so that it cannot be upside down. Is it upside down? Did it know what it had to grasp, or not? It knew. What about the feet? If the toes were attached at the back instead of the front, could you walk? Think about it. The nose hairs knew there was dust in the air, the eyes knew there was a sun, and the mouth knew there was food.

Because of that love, even death can be overcome. When that love explodes, it generates the power to overcome any difficulty. Do you understand this? 
That core existence of love is God. In order for humans to become relative beings resembling this God, they must possess a nature that can correspond to God’s nature. In electrical principles, plus and minus become one, but plus and plus, minus and minus repel each other, right? Why do they repel? It is not that they are destined to repel from the beginning. There are times when they will repel. Look, when a downpour is about to come, dark clouds gather and rumble, right? That is the principle. What causes that? It is due to electrical action. The plus power and minus power, which are in the billions of volts, long for each other and collide, producing light. Love also shines.

Then does the plus power equivalent to billions of volts suddenly burst out? No. Small pluses unite in a joint offensive. It is not that a large plus emerges all at once; rather, small pluses combine to form a large plus domain. Wouldn't a great plus domain not be formed without passing through the total sum of pluses? That theory is correct, right? If I had not become a teacher in the Unification Church, I would have become a doctor with this.

So how do pluses combine to create a great plus? This is the problem. You must understand this. A minus must arise before a plus can arise, but if a plus arises before a minus, those pluses will combine. When plus and minus are about to collide, if another plus arises just before, those pluses will combine. Then the minus will follow. It will follow even if it is just a fraction of a billion. In this way, pluses combine to form a complete plus domain, and when an equal minus domain is formed, it shines. Do you understand?

Once a minus is determined before a plus, when like poles meet, they repel each other. This makes sense, right? Before marriage, bachelors can unite with other bachelors. Also, before marriage, maidens can unite with other maidens. However, when a counterpart appears, it is different. If an unattractive woman marries a handsome man, she does not like her beautiful friends lingering around her husband. She dislikes it when her friends come over. That is rebellion. Isn't that true? This makes sense, right? This is logical.

What is the reason for this? You must understand that. Why? According to the principle, a being that does not have a foundation to completely give and receive cannot endure. It will cease to exist. The existence of plus and minus resembles God's eternal form, which can endure together, but if either the minus or plus is alone, it will cease to exist. Therefore, do not be indecisive; create a counterpart to endure.

The heavens and the earth, the world of all actions, are formed by the actions of repulsion and fusion. If the repulsive action were to repel forever, that would be a contradiction. Imprisonment in North Korea
The teacher was imprisoned in a North Korean communist prison for 2 years and 8 months, doing hard labor. What kind of labor? It was work at a fertilizer factory. Ammonium sulfate was transported on a conveyor belt to fall in the middle of the factory. The task was to weigh it and fill it into bags to load onto carts. 

Since it was produced through heat treatment, the falling ammonium sulfate was hot. If it cools down, it becomes clumpy. If left for several years, it turns into something as hard as rock. It was truly grueling hard labor. Each person had a responsibility in the 8-hour workday. Ten people formed a team. The daily responsibility for one team was 1,300 bags, and if they did not finish within 8 hours, their food would be halved. The daily ration was about 1.7 bowls of rice in a small bowl. There were no side dishes, and the soup was just saltwater, not miso soup. They worked for 8 hours on that. 

The communist strategy was to work people to death. After three years in such conditions, everyone dies. It is certain, without a doubt. Within three years. Because they are forced to work hard without food, those who enter this factory are essentially already dead. 

By the standards of ordinary people in this world, even with three meals a day, the maximum one could do is 700 bags. However, this factory requires much more than that. The food is so little that just a few bites are enough. And then, doing hard labor, one stumbles on the way to the factory after eating breakfast. It is truly a miserable situation. 

Victory of the Spirit
The teacher was quite aware of the communist policies, so he was careful not to get caught. He decided to live on only half of the food provided. Humans do not live by bread alone; they live by the word of God. In any case, this food would lead to death. So, it took him half a month to resolve to live on just half of the food. He ate half and shared the other half. How happy he felt mentally! The question was how much emotional nourishment he could gain each day. Spiritual comfort is indeed significant. 

Life is scientific. Even while working, one does not consciously think about the labor. The working hours were prayer hours. He always imagined various global matters. He left the prison at 8 AM and arrived at the factory by 10 AM. He was given 10 minutes to go to the bathroom. He was already exhausted to the point of wanting to die. He felt a pain that could melt his stomach. Yet, he did not think about the work at all. Once he started thinking about it, he could only imagine the rest time. Lifting 40 kg of refined material was the most painful task. Everyone hated it. The teacher took on this difficult task that everyone else avoided. 

Continuing this hard work would lead to death. Therefore, the only way to survive was to build the stamina to carry out this hardest task. You should also take on the most difficult tasks. Think progressively. 

Since they had to transport more than 1,300 bags a day, there was no time to rest. 1,300 bags would be a mountain larger than this auditorium (Sutaek-ri). Just think about it. 1,300 bags. This had to be done within 8 hours. It took 5 to 10 minutes to fill the bags and move them. On average, it took 5 minutes to finish. Others took 15 minutes. With such time consumption, one could not fulfill their responsibility. Since they were digging into a mountain, moving the scale more than 4 to 5 meters would delay them. So, he researched a method to minimize movement. 

Since everyone else did not follow this method, he had to do it alone. By doing so, since everyone has a conscience, the teacher was able to handle more than half of the 1,300 bags alone, and they followed suit. The teacher was a model worker. He received the model worker award from the communist party every year. At that time, his weight was 72 kg (19 gwon 300). Now, it is close to 81 kg (21 gwon). Although he may not look like much on the outside, he had weight in his bones. While others were losing weight, the teacher did not. So, he became the subject of everyone's study. 

He educated newcomers. The body suffers from lactic acid. Hair falls out, and if you squeeze the skin, water comes out. After six months, one must have a breakdown. Generally, people think they have tuberculosis and become discouraged, leading to death. They can only endure for a year and a half or two at most. 

How Hungry Are You?
How hungry are you? How much do you want to eat? It cannot be expressed in words. When family or someone visits, they bring something, and no matter how much you love your wife or miss your mother, your eyes go to the things they brought before looking at their faces. You can eat what they bring during visits. The joy of being able to eat something is greater than seeing the long-missed wife or mother. Since food is rarely given in the factory, if food is not provided during visits, it becomes a social issue, so this was allowed. 

There has never been a time as sad as when someone comes to visit without bringing powdered grain. It is said to be sadder than losing a parent. This may be hard for you to understand. How hungry can one be? When you are hungry, gastric juices naturally flow. The stomach starts to move, and you feel feverish. Therefore, saliva drips like gum. You probably cannot even imagine that. The most longed-for thing is to eat to your heart's content. If that could happen, one would think it would be fine to die. That is how precious food was. It was a continuous series of such days. If someone came to visit and brought powdered grain, they would knead it to make rice cakes. However, if they knead it with a stone, the powder sticks to the stone, so they do not use stones much. If powder sticks to the stone, they would immediately compete to eat it. It is beyond words to express. 

How much do you long for food? It is a longing that surpasses the point of death. When one cannot go to the factory, their food is inevitably halved. The communist rule is that those who do not work should not eat. Even if one is sick, they long for a bowl of rice just like everyone else and do their utmost to go out. Then, with their last strength, they work and come back to eat dinner, dying in the process. When that happens, those around them will fight to take away the food of the deceased. 

The teacher studied deeply about humanity in such circumstances. Just as he longed for food, he wondered if he longed for God in the same way. The teacher lived each day comparing and contrasting. "Above all, I must love God. I did not come here just to eat this piece of rice. I came to pave the way for the restoration of all humanity." He never adopted an attitude of distrust toward his own work. That is why the teacher became well-known. 

And he absolutely did not speak. Knowing the organization of the communist party, he understood that even without speaking, they would cooperate from the spiritual world. As long as one lives for a purpose, there is nothing to worry about. God mobilizes all means and methods to help. The teacher always wore the oldest clothes. He gave the good ones to others, and when they wore out...
create a new world. Therefore, the suffering that we experience is not merely a burden but a pathway to a greater purpose.

The True Meaning of the Holy Wine Ceremony
The reason for the Holy Wine Ceremony and its significance
You must resolve the lineage that has been defiled due to the fall and restore the original good lineage of creation. If you do not completely resolve the 6,000 years of history and undergo the process of indemnity and restoration, you cannot reach the blessing. The engagement ceremony must occur because Adam and Eve must return to the state before the fall at the engagement stage. The lineage inherited from the fall must be transformed. If this is not done, one cannot escape original sin, and without escaping original sin, one cannot rise to the stage of being blessed as true children. This is how the principle works. The transformation of lineage to escape the original sin caused by the fall, that is, the exchange of blood, is the Holy Wine Ceremony.

When viewed from the perspective of Jesus, this Holy Wine Ceremony is similar to the Last Supper. In the Last Supper, bread is eaten and wine is drunk instead of flesh and blood. This signifies that because we humans have fallen, we must receive the body of Jesus, meaning we must undergo a new incarnation. Likewise, this Holy Wine Ceremony is performed because humans must return in the opposite direction of the path of the fall.

On October 18, 1970, at the Central Training Center.
* This message was given during the Holy Wine Ceremony for 235 Japanese couples before the joint wedding ceremony of 777 couples, and it has been translated from the second issue of the publication "Blessing" issued by the Japanese Association.

The fall was committed through the archangel and Eve, so the restoration begins with Chairman Kim, who stands in the position of the restored archangel. One cannot return without going through Adam before the fall. One must return to the parents. One must pass through such a path. One must return to the seed of life within the unfallen Adam. Only by returning to that standard can one formally enter the realm of resurrection.

It is done centered on love. Because the fall occurred centered on love, one must also be restored centered on love. For us to be restored, we must return to the womb, but in reality, that is not possible. Therefore, we establish a condition of restoration centered on love. One must return to the restored Adam and unite with him to receive the lineage.

In the beginning, Eve fell spiritually centered on Satan. Then, she became one with Adam and fell physically. Therefore, to restore this, the Holy Wine Ceremony is performed to welcome the completely restored Adam and become one spiritually. It is a ceremony to restore the bond of love. Such a condition must be established. By becoming one spiritually and returning to God, the woman becomes the one who restores the man in reality, which is the wedding ceremony.

Contents of the Holy Wine
What is contained in the Holy Wine is something that symbolizes parental love. And it must contain something that symbolizes blood. Therefore, by drinking it, one becomes one with parental love and also one with the blood. This is the content of the Holy Wine. Then, how is the Holy Wine made? It is made from wine that symbolizes the earth, the sea, and the sky, and symbolizes the whole. The Holy Wine contains three types of wine. In addition, it contains symbols of all things. To drink this means to be spiritually born and physically born.

Without this ceremony, one cannot escape original sin and transform the lineage. If the lineage is not transformed, one cannot pass the standard of completion and become one with God's love. Therefore, one must understand that the Holy Wine Ceremony is a ceremony of indemnity for all of this.

The order is from Chairman Kubo of the Japanese Association to Chairman Kim (the restored archangel), then to Teacher Choi Won-bok, who stands in the position of a fallen world’s restored Cain-like mother, and finally to the position of the True Mother, who is unfallen. Before performing the Holy Wine Ceremony, the teacher places his hands on the hands of the women, signifying unity. By doing so, they become one spiritually. Through this, the purpose of receiving the teacher's body is established, and one becomes one with the counterpart in spirit and flesh. Thus, while until now one has been in the position of a daughter, now they are spiritually in the position of the counterpart.

One must pass through such a position as one body. Therefore, the counterpart is in the position of a mother for three years. This is the content of the Holy Wine Ceremony that will be performed from now on.

**Holy Wedding Ceremony and Bloodline Restoration**
The joint wedding ceremony conducted centered around our Unification Church is not limited to the Unification Church alone. It is a formal path that all humanity must inevitably go through. We must understand this clearly.

**The Reason We Must Receive Blessing**
So, what is the fundamental reason for this? It is because our human ancestors fell. If our human ancestors had not fallen, we would not be experiencing such blessings today. However, due to the fall, a path of restoration remains that requires us to return to God's dominion. This is why people today believe in religion, and it is also why history is progressing in this direction.

Ultimately, what is the final purpose? It is to find true families. This is the highest goal that fallen humanity seeks. To establish this true family, true individuals must emerge. Among true love, true men must come forth first. Thus, that true man must find and establish a true woman, and through the marriage centered on God, the true family will finally emerge.

Because humanity fell, we could not have such origins, so we must deny all past families and step over this familial standard according to God's providential will. If we cannot step over that standard, fallen humanity cannot return to the original world, according to principle. Fallen humans must understand that they cannot stand before God without going through this formal condition.

**The Significance of Engagement Ceremony, Holy Wedding Ceremony, and Marriage Ceremony**
After you have the engagement ceremony, there is the Holy Wedding Ceremony, and then the marriage ceremony. So, what are these engagement ceremony, Holy Wedding Ceremony, and marriage ceremony? They are not ceremonies conducted according to any precedent. They are inevitable events that symbolically reenact all the fallen content in order to indemnify it.

At what stage did Adam and Eve fall? They fell at the engagement stage. In other words, they fell during the process of growing toward the goal of completion. Then, what is the purpose of engagement? It is marriage. Because Adam and Eve fell at the stage of engagement due to a flawed marriage, we must deny that flawed marriage and correct it anew centered on God. However, we cannot simply deny this in any way. We must have content that opposes the fallen content.

The ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, fell due to their wrongful love centered on themselves. By involving the archangel in their love for each other, they expelled God and the original true personality of Adam and the original true personality of Eve. By introducing a love relationship that God did not permit, what arose in humanity is original sin. Therefore, the issue for us humans is to shed this original sin. However, since we were born from false parents, we cannot shed this original sin without reenacting the love relationship of true parents.

In our Unification Principle, what are we trying to achieve centered around the expectations of faith and substantial expectations? We are trying to return to the position of the engagement stage before the fall. Since the stage just before the fall is the engagement stage, we must return to the position of Adam and Eve before they fell. So, how do we return to the engagement stage before the fall?

Adam and Eve fell through false love and became false parents, and centered on these false parents, their three sons Cain, Abel, and Seth, along with their wives, all fell. Therefore, the content to restore the form of these eight people inside and out is precisely the expectations of faith and substantial expectations. After restoring this, we must go over to embrace the Heavenly Parents.

Here, who are the Heavenly Parents? They are the Messiah. Therefore, after passing through the substantial expectations, there must be an expectation for the Messiah. Without the Messiah before fallen humanity, we cannot return to the original position. The descendants of fallen Adam and Eve cannot shed original sin without welcoming the Messiah.

So, who is that Messiah? True Parents. Then why are True Parents necessary? Because they must perform the work of grafting us back through their love. Thus, without the appearing of the Messiah, True Parents, fallen humanity cannot shed original sin and cannot move to a position where they can receive the blessing of completion in a sinless liberated state. Therefore, the engagement ceremony is a ceremony to restore the fall of humanity's ancestors Adam and Eve at the engagement stage. The Holy Wedding Ceremony is to extract the blood of Satan that has been defiled due to the fall. In other words, it is a ceremony to remove original sin.

Those with original sin cannot come to the position of blessing. Because they carry the bloodline of Satan within them, they have no way to enter the position of blessing centered on God. Therefore, we must absolutely settle the original sin. This original sin was established through the love of false parents, so to settle this, we must establish conditions of indemnity centered on the love of True Parents to step over it. Without shedding this original sin, there can be no blessing centered on God's love in the position of completed couples.

You who are engaged will have the Holy Wedding Ceremony before the blessing ceremony on the 21st, which is a ceremony for changing the bloodline. Fallen humanity cannot enter the position of blessing without denying all past love that has been defiled by the false love of the world of Satan and without establishing a resurrection-like substance centered on God's love to reenact the love of True Parents. Therefore, the Holy Wedding Ceremony is a ceremony that promises to establish a new standard of life through the gateway of True Parents' love.

Life is born from the foundation of love, so you must become one centered on the love of True Parents. Otherwise, you cannot have a history of resurrection. That is why we go through this three-stage process.

**7-Year Course**  
The teacher established the Three-Stage Foundation. It is not centered on each individual but on the teacher. In fact, it is better to create the Three-Stage Foundation centered on the children of one's faith. Internally, it centers on the teacher and establishes a parent-child relationship. That is the meaning behind the creation of the Three-Stage Foundation.  

**Why Must We Evangelize 12 People?**  
For three years, one must be active. During that time, one must evangelize more than 12 people. Jesus had 12 disciples. The 12 represent those who restore Jacob's lineage in Israel.  

Therefore, among the Israelite people centered on Jacob, there were 70 elders. They represent the national Israel. Originally, there were 72. The 72 is six times 12. When combined, it enters the 7 stages. Thus, without restoring the 72, tribal restoration cannot occur.  

To determine an eternal foundation of rest for one's family that is not invaded from the outside, one must restore 12 families. The Three-Stage Foundation is like the qualifications to pass through the three doors of the East to enter heaven. Therefore, to enter heaven, one must serve 12 people and obtain the victory rights that subjugate them. For that reason, it took Jesus three years to gather the 12 disciples and achieve heartistic unity, but he ultimately failed. One cannot restore unless one stands in a position that respects the children of faith more than their own life. The Unification Church is currently restoring under such conditions. Therefore, at least 12 people must be evangelized.  

The idea of centering on three people means that when there is a center, the directions of east, west, south, and north are determined, but only one entrance from the east is allowed among those directions. The sun rises in the east. Therefore, in the spirit world, the east signifies spring. It is a position that has obtained spring. For spring to come again, it must pass through summer, autumn, and winter. Thus, to stand in a position that is never slandered by Satan, the standard of completing the 12 must be established.  

If one thinks this way, the problem lies in the three months of standing in the winter position. Those three months correspond to the three days during which Jesus was crucified. From spring to summer, autumn, winter, and then to a new spring, it has developed in a spiral. Therefore, during these three years, at least 12 must be evangelized.  

One must not be with their spouse. One must not be with their husband either. Age does not matter. These three years symbolize the entire stage. This period is when one renews and sanctifies the family that was lost.

Where humans should originally dwell

Just as it cannot be denied that a new history is created from there, you must understand that the laws of heaven are established only through such a process.

Your families should not end with just being families. Before you lies the enormous goal of forming tribes centered around the family. Only when families are completely united can they stand before the tribe. If they cannot unite, they will stand in a position of avoiding the tribe. Until today, humanity has not understood this. Thinking that everything would be resolved if men did their part and women did theirs, they have struggled until now. This must not be the case. Individuals and families must stand in a position where they share a common purpose, and only then can God accompany them. Moreover, only when they have the content to do so can they dominate humanity.

This is because descendants come forth based on a familial foundation, and therefore there must be a value-centered connection between men and women based on heart. Only when such a bond is established can they become an object of admiration for all people. Only then can they dominate the world. This is indispensable. That is why the term "True Parents" spoken of in the Unification Church is a great term. Of course, the content of truth is profound, but the term "True Parents" is indeed a great term.

From here, the starting point for the future is guaranteed. It can guarantee certainty and value regarding the future. Furthermore, if there is a point of origin that can guarantee value in the reality stage, it comes from that term.

Establish a family centered on parental love. What should we do here? We must unite. Who should we unite around? We must not unite around ourselves. We must not try to unite with True Parents centered on our own families. We must be drawn to True Parents. In being drawn, it is not just oneself that is drawn; parents, husbands, wives, and even children must be drawn along. Moreover, even the material possessions in the family must be drawn along. Only then can we unite.

When we look at historical eras, the Old Testament era was centered around material, while the New Testament era was centered around love. Jesus spoke of love, but humanity did not know what love was. In the Old Testament era, offerings were made for atonement. Without offerings, there could be no gratitude. Thus, one must go through the process of offering. Here, what is the offering? It is a sacrificial offering. That is why, in the Old Testament era, everything was offered as a sacrificial offering in place of humanity, along with animals as offerings. We understand that this was the time of the Old Testament.

Then, Jesus introduced a higher level of God's love. In the Old Testament era, Moses could not introduce the loving God but only the God of power, the God of might, and the God of judgment. However, Jesus introduced the God of love. He introduced the loving Jesus, but the people of that time did not accept it.

Through this process, we have come to this point. What we must understand here is that we must center on parents. Love cannot manifest without parents. People must be born from parents to give and receive love. Without this relational standard, love cannot be achieved.

All things exist for the sake of humanity. What does the entire history culminate in? It culminates in the standards of material, children, and parents, in other words, the family. This is the foundation of the universe. Without parents, children cannot be born. Children born from parents must govern all things centered on their parents. Adam and Eve must also govern all things. This applies to everything at once.

When you decide to live to fulfill your purpose, you cannot do it alone. You must gather all these contents and move forward. When this gathered content is pressed down, it becomes a single point. Isn’t that right? When it is compressed, it becomes a single point. If this single point divides into two, conflict arises.

Vertical history must be compensated horizontally. When viewed in three dimensions, what does history correspond to for you? It corresponds to the family. The family is the historical center.

The goal of all revolutions to present hope before the future world is not the nation. It is not the world. While there have been those who presented revolutionary views of nations and the world in this historical process, there has been no subject force that has presented a revolutionary view of the family to establish a new framework for the family.

So what does the Unification Church aim to do? There cannot be a tribal revolution before there is a family revolution, nor can there be a national revolution before there is a tribal revolution, nor can there be a world revolution before there is a national revolution. Therefore, it aims to achieve a family revolution along with the completion of the individual.

Revolution cannot be achieved without discarding and breaking down the existing. Without removing the past, new things cannot be achieved. Therefore, one must deny oneself, deny one’s family, and deny one’s possessions. This is essential.

The family is the foundation of the universe. Jesus did not say to love your children. He said to love God before loving your children. He instructed to love God more than oneself. That is why Jesus said, “You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your mind. This is the first commandment.”

We, as humans, do not have the root of life, so we must be grafted onto the root. Should we be blown about like a dandelion in the wind? It means we have no root. This may sound harsh, but in the fallen world, which absolutely requires such environmental conditions, it is a message of the gospel that cannot be spoken lightly.

So how should we love God? Should we place Him in the palace of paradise, or should we let Him wander? We have been struggling to find a way to shift from a heavenly center to a life-centered approach. Until now, there has been no way to shift the human world to a life-centered approach, so such a way must exist. What this means is that there must be a true subject of love centered on God's love.

When viewed from the perspective of a nation, if the king of the nation is seen as the father, then the people are in the position of sons, and the land is in the position of all things. The basic unit that condenses this is the family. Therefore, everything belonging to the father and the son in the family must be offered to God. Others may say they will offer only their children and possessions, excluding themselves. This will not lead to the overall restoration.

So where is the foundation you must advance on behalf of the nation? Where is the altar of the nation? It is the family. Loving the nation is not to take away from the nation but to give more to it. People do not understand this. Why is the Republic of Korea corrupt today? To deny something does not mean to end with the denial but to exchange it for something greater. We are well aware of this reality.

Finding parents makes it easy to find children and all things. Everything is positioned as parents, children, and all things. In today’s world, children follow their parents, and all things follow the children. The greater is centered around the lesser, supporting the parents. We must carry this forward even to the world of eternity. We must lead even to the world of death in this fallen reality. Parents must lead their children. When born as children, they are already prepared to become parents. Therefore, around the parents, the children must be gathered. So do you have the desire to eternally surround the teacher of the Unification Church? This is the question.
