How to live a life of gratitude

Then the question is whether you are living a life of gratitude. How do you express gratitude? When you see someone with many children, you might think that person has a lot of hardships, but you must understand that they feel a happiness that those without children cannot experience. Those who have raised children will know this. When comparing those who have raised children and those who have not, those who have raised children feel a sense of fulfillment in life, no matter how complicated their children may be, while those without children cannot feel that.

It is through children that one feels the fulfillment of life. Just because the environment is complicated does not mean one is unhappy. There is hope for tomorrow intertwined in that. The more sons and daughters one has that others do not, the more one can have new hopes in various fields, thus overcoming their difficult circumstances.

When looking at this, the question becomes how to live a life of gratitude. You are always dealing with material. However, you should think about feeding not just your children with that material but also feeding the nation and the world. When you deal with material, even if it is small, if you have the intention to give it for the world and are sincere, and compare that to someone who clings to that material to leave it for their children, how do you think God would view that?

You must understand that goodness is always a public stance. No matter how small the material is, if it is offered sincerely for God, it can be used to enter the world. You must understand this. When a person who has only one hundred won stakes that hundred won on God's love, that hundred won represents the whole and their character.

Even a small piece of land cannot be called my property. Everything is received from God. Since it is received from God, it must be returned. No matter how small it is, since it is received from God, it must be returned to God in a valuable way. When that happens, history unfolds. Since it has been received in that way, one must become a giver in that way. If a world of such people does not exist, this earth cannot become heaven.

In the 24 hours of daily life, everything I see, hear, and do is for what purpose? It is for God. You must see and hear for God. You must also feel for God. Although we live on earth, we must connect our lives to the heavenly world. Those who cannot live in the heavenly world cannot grasp the heavenly world, can they?

A filial child is called so because they have lived much connected to their parents' love, and a loyal subject is called so because they have made great efforts to unify their entire life with the nation. You must understand this.

When you give and receive an object, it must be as a part of the world. How much do you feel and embody this fact in your life? Some of you may think, "Ah! I have believed in the Unification Church for decades, but I have become such a pitiful being." That is a mistaken thought.

Who do you give for? And who do you receive for? You must give for God and receive for God. Since you received for God, you must give for God. Since you gave for God, you should not say you will receive for yourself.

That is why Jesus Christ prayed, "Not my will, but Yours be done," even in suffering. However, fallen humans would have prayed for themselves in that position. They would have wanted to receive for themselves. Fallen humans are different.

Be ashamed when you give and be humble when you receive.

Who should you center your giving and receiving around? You must center it around God. You must give and receive public things, not private ones. If you have given something to someone centered on God, does God want to give you only that, or does He want to give you something greater, feeling pained in His heart, and feeling ashamed while giving? That is the issue. Parents do not boast when they give; rather, they feel ashamed even while giving.

Parents feel ashamed and pained when they cannot give their children as much as others, even though they want to give more. When they see their child crying, they naturally feel tears in their hearts. That is public. A child born from such a parent will become a wonderful child. Since that child was born publicly, they must live giving and receiving for the world. A person who has the mindset of feeling ashamed when giving and feels humble and grateful when receiving is a person living a life of gratitude. Through such people, new history unfolds, and through such content, heaven is established, which you must clearly understand.

Today, many members of our Unification Church have engaged in international marriages that cross borders. Many have married people with whom they cannot communicate at all. They invest their entire lives and youth in marrying those who cannot communicate. Who are they investing this precious youth for, which only happens once? It is to break down the walls of enmity that the world has built as borders. Therefore, we must first create a foundation where this nation and other nations can unite through the path of suffering and twists. Such people possess an authority that no one from that nation or any motive from that nation's history can dominate, and they can unify the world of enmity. In this sense, we should respect and praise them as noble people. If there are those who can say thank you while walking the path of suffering and can lament their own shortcomings afterward, these individuals will conquer the world and dominate ideologies. You must understand this.

Therefore, you should shed tears and be grateful in the position you are in. You should be thankful to God for what you have received that you did not even hope for, despite being insufficient. A person who feels ashamed when receiving and has the mindset to feel ashamed while giving will never fail. Just wait and see. You must understand that such a person cannot help but live a life of gratitude.

If Adam and Eve had received God's command not to eat with gratitude and lived with the mindset of "How can such a high and precious being speak to us, who are ashamed?" and acted cautiously, they would not have fallen. Our Resolve on the Day of Children
Today is October 30th in the solar calendar and the 1st of October in the lunar calendar, the 11th Day of Children. You may know that this Day of Children was established exactly ten years ago. This marks the 11th occurrence. 

The History of Humanity Seeking a True Adam
Originally, days such as God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day were meant to be observed not over the course of a year but on a single day. However, because humanity fell into the unfortunate condition of the Fall, we could not observe them on a single day, and God has worked hard until now to find such days. 

If humanity had not fallen, the Day of Parents and the Day of Children would have been established along with the perfection of humanity, and at the same time, God's wishes would have been fulfilled. In other words, the ideal of creation would have been perfected. Moreover, if the perfected creation and the perfected Adam and Eve had completely united centered on God's love, a triangular relationship would have formed where God and humanity could not be separated, and humanity and all things could not be separated, achieving oneness. However, due to the Fall of humanity, God's love was lost, and we lost the day to commemorate true parents, true children, and true all things. 

To restore this day, we must go through a sorrowful path of restoration and a painful path of re-creation. In the process of re-creation, all things must be re-created centered on humanity, and God's ideal of creation and God's love must be re-created centered on humanity. This process of restoration remains. God has worked hard until now to restore this. 

Looking at the historical process to find all things, all things were already in a position invaded by Satan, so it was necessary to separate Satan. Therefore, a history of separating Satan was conducted centered on the condition of offerings. This was done in the Old Testament era. When entering the New Testament era, God sought to find humanity, but since we humans have fallen bloodlines, a history of separation was absolutely necessary. 

Thus, on the foundation of the victory of separation, a new couple must go through the process of the confrontation between God's love and Satan's love, and God's love must remain there. Only then can we meet the day of wishes that heaven desires. 

We know well how tedious this historical process has been. In order to lay the foundation for the victory where God's love can be reborn on such a day, countless sacrifices have been made throughout history. In that process, all things have groaned, and many prophets and saints have paid the price of blood and death to return to humanity. We know that we have come to find a true Adam by gathering and gathering the price of such sacrifices. 

Establishing the figure of Adam and working through the ages to find the completed image of Adam has been the history of the past 6,000 years. After finding Adam, we must find Eve. Only after finding Eve can we finally fulfill the complete will and complete God's ideal of creation. Individuals who can complete the ideal of creation must establish true marital relationships and, through unity with God's love, complete the dominion of goodness. 

However, we cannot do this with just the standard of "very good." You all know that without the involvement of God's love, we cannot see completion according to the principles. 

If we examine history, the Old Testament era was the time to distinguish all things, the New Testament era was the time to distinguish people, and the era of the New Covenant is the time to distinguish the families of love that Adam and Eve lost, centered on the victorious Adam and Eve. This era is the era of completion. In other words, because humanity lost its parents, we must distinguish centered on the parents of humanity. For these parents to come to this earth and go through the process of distinction, they cannot avoid a path of suffering. This is a principled view. 

What We Must Reflect on as We Celebrate the Day of Children
God has worked for 2,000 years centered on Christianity. It has been the wish of Christians to become the sons and daughters of God. What is the responsibility of those sons and daughters? It was to fulfill the duty of filial piety to the coming parents. If they had fulfilled this duty, the parents could have avoided the path of humiliation. However, because they failed to fulfill that responsibility, the parents found themselves in a position of taking on the responsibilities of their children. 

Today’s Unification Church must fulfill both the duties of children and parents. We know that we have gone through a historical process of several decades centered on this. Thus, today, on the 1st of October in the lunar calendar, we celebrate the 11th Day of Children. 

Let us examine the historical process leading up to this Day of Children. When viewed centered on the Israelite people, the mission of Judaism was to fulfill filial piety before the parents by taking on the responsibility of direct children from the position of adopted children. They should have completely honored Jesus as their parent, considering his will more important than their own lives. If the foundation of Judaism had been established to fulfill the rights of children, there would have been no path of death for Jesus. If that had been the case, the children could have prevented the suffering of their parent before Jesus underwent suffering. 

Children have the responsibility to block the path of death for their parents and fulfill the duty of filial piety. Therefore, if Judaism had fulfilled its responsibilities as children, Jesus would not have had to face death and would have fulfilled God's will. However, Judaism not only failed to fulfill the responsibilities of children but also betrayed their parent, Jesus, and drove him to the path of death. As a result, God set a standard for the providence of spiritual salvation and has worked to spiritually gather the children, establishing a foundation for global development. That global foundation is Christianity. 

Here, while the spiritual foundation of children has been laid centered on Christianity, it has not been sufficient with just the spiritual standard. Therefore, God has worked hard until now to establish an external standard that can align with this standard. Thus, we know that the democratic world has been created centered on the spirit and body. The ideological center of this democratic world, which is the providential center, is Christianity, and it must fulfill the duties of true filial piety and loyalty before the coming parents. As heavenly parents or heavenly lords, when they come to this earth to fulfill their will, they must be able to devote everything without holding back. If Christianity had established such a foundation, there would have been no path of suffering before the coming parents.

May the entire purpose of the restoration providence for which you have worked for the world be allowed to reach the final victory day, centered on your love. 

Father, may your children, who have been protected through countless sufferings and adversities, and who have been nurtured in a lonely place where no one knows, greet a bright new morning and be able to serve you and praise you in a free environment. 

We have come out knowing that such a day will come, and we have fought for that time until now. When we think again about why we are here and what we have gathered for, it is to find new individuals, new families, new tribes, new nations, and a new world. We have gathered to seek a new world to serve you anew. We also gather with the desire to become new filial sons and daughters who can serve your joyful form. 

Father, in the past, we were not in a position where we could serve you freely. Our environment was not a free world where your sons and daughters could reveal their authority, nor was it your nation. They were not your tribes, your families, or your individuals. We longed for such things infinitely, but we were sad people who had lost everything. We must understand that overcoming this sad self is the path of struggle, the path of indemnity, and the path of restoration. 

You sacrificed individuals to find new families, and you sacrificed those families to find new tribes, and you sacrificed those tribes to find new nations, and you sacrificed those nations to advance to a new world. Furthermore, we must recognize that the limit of restoration, which requires sacrificing that nation, is still connected before us. 

Father, we must remember that we are a people without a nation, a people without a tribal authority, a people without a family, and a people who have forgotten themselves. We must keep in mind this sad and painful fact that we are your sons and daughters serving you. 

We must be prepared to overcome our bodies and dedicate everything to establish the victorious nation you seek. Father, this morning, command us. Now our hearts must be anxious, and our bodies must hurry toward one direction. We must realize that we should prepare ourselves and go, and we must run toward the distant road of tomorrow. It is not only our responsibility to walk the path we must take but also our responsibility to trace the path of pioneers. We must recognize this sad situation. 

We must understand that joy, glory, and shouts are not waiting for us ahead, but rather struggles, lamentations, and undeveloped territories that must be pioneered.

<Words> Today is November 1st. This morning, I want to tell you one thing: we must surely prepare good individuals to form a good nation and family, to establish a good tribe, and to create a good nation, as we are messengers who have received a heavenly mission.  
To leave the results of truth  
Leaving behind true goodness is not a simple task. Throughout the historical process, countless people have pursued goodness and sought a nation of goodness, but they have not yet achieved it, and we are reminded of the historical legacy left to us. Knowing God, understanding the historical process, knowing what the mission given in this era is, and knowing how the future world will conclude, we must absolutely achieve this purpose of goodness.  
Truth does not arise by chance. Truth must have a motive and go through a process to emerge. Without that, the results of truth will not appear. Who should be the motive of that truth? It must be either God or man. Nothing else can be the motive of truth. A third condition cannot be connected to us as the motive of truth. Considering this, God must guide and lead us humans from a true position, or we must serve God from a true position. Otherwise, we must understand that we cannot form true individuals, true families, true nations, or true countries that we desire.  
We know that many great figures who have come and gone in history fought to become true people and dedicated their lives for that purpose. Their desire to become true people was not merely to leave behind their true selves. They walked the path of suffering and pioneers, hoping for the day when true humanity would become a true race and a true world, establishing a relationship with that true self, as we know well through history.  
Thus, truth must always have a motive and be manifested through a process. Until now, the motive of truth has been God. There is a distance to cover to inherit that motive and go through the process to achieve the result. The question is, who will connect that? God can be the motive, but we know well through principles that He cannot directly lead the process to achieve the result. Then, who must bear the responsibility in this process? It must be humanity.  
The many saints and sages who have come to this earth have pursued truth and fought for goodness, and their path was not a smooth one but a path of suffering. Why was that? They had to maintain truth and connect it to the era and living environment while leaving it behind. However, the living environment and conditions were not conducive to absorb truth. Therefore, conflict must have arisen. In other words, the surrounding environment was not in a position to welcome truth on its path, so it could not proceed smoothly and had to go through a process of struggle.  
The world we live in is a world of sin. Furthermore, the history of humanity, based on the premise of the fall, is a history governed by evil. Therefore, for goodness to flourish in an environment where evil holds all authority, it could not avoid the path of indemnification. So, where should we start to expand the foundation of goodness? We must start from the individual. To do that, we must engage in personal struggles. Thus, we must develop into families, tribes, nations, and the world.  
For this reason, God, who is the origin of the motive, has always bestowed the motive of goodness upon us humans. "You must become the people of the new nation. You must become the good people of the new era." He has always sought to provide us with the motive of goodness through great figures, sages, or saints in every era. We must understand that God will continue to hold onto the connections of motives until the end of history, guiding humanity through the providence of living within a century.  
Therefore, history may seem to unfold without connections, but the underlying motive comes from God and is connected through relationships. Based on this relationship, the current Christian cultural sphere has been established around the new realm of goodness centered on Israel.  
From this perspective, the time when the motivational content, the process of humanity, and the resulting purpose can be unified is precisely the time of our hoped-for desires and the end times of human history. Such a time must surely come.  
The motive, process, and result must be compressed so that the motive appears as a result, and the process connects with both the motive and the result, allowing my individual self to stand in a position to thank God and praise His victory. Otherwise, we cannot complete the personality of the individual we desire. We cannot restore the personality of the true individual we wish for. We must understand that we are racing towards that goal.  
A true person must appear who embodies the alignment of the motive, process, and result centered on truth  
Before the historical end times, there must first be personal end times for the motive, process, and result centered on truth to bear fruit in your individual selves. God has been seeking that true center, that true human, looking forward to that time. This is the concept of the Messiah.

Furthermore, it is an existence that cannot be exchanged for the results found at the boundary of the sorrow of indemnification that must be covered globally in this fallen world. You must understand that you must become such a valuable existence.  
What does this mean? It means that you must always be a center that can rise as an object of praise and joy in the heart of God, who is the motive. You must become a central being equipped with valuable content that can represent and exceed these three values. By becoming the center of this new horizontal world, you must bring forth a new result that has gone through a process without struggle and without contradictions or conflicts. This can be seen as the union of God's desires, the desires of all humanity, and the desires of the entire history.  
Where will such a position begin? Of course, it will start from an individual and from a specific place. However, what will be the content that begins? Without God's love, true motives cannot be established, true processes cannot be inherited, and true results cannot be brought forth. When we think about this, ultimately what remains is God's love.  
God's love is not the kind of love that humans speak of today. It is a love that encompasses and surpasses everything. The results must not be for one's individual self but must become the center of love that can be seen by the whole, become the factor of life for the whole, and be beneficial for all. This is God's love. The center of all motives, the center of the process, and the center of the result is God's love. **Sincerity Moves Heaven**  
Absolute truth must go through an absolute process to be found. Therefore, to seek it, suffering must be exhausted. Personal suffering, familial suffering, tribal suffering, national suffering, and global suffering must be exhausted for global peace to come.

Moreover, when we say "sincerity moves heaven," is sincerity easy? It is not easy. Sincerity is putting forth effort with the resolve to face death.

What is the limit of sincerity? What is the highest form of sincerity? If one puts forth sincerity for their own happiness, they may achieve their personal desires, but that sincerity cannot fulfill the will of the world. Is sincerity for the nation the limit? It may be sincerity for the nation, but nothing beyond that. The limit of sincerity is to fulfill the will of the world.

One must put forth sincerity for the world. Then, why do we put forth sincerity for the world? It is to fulfill God's will. What purpose does God's will have? While it includes the will for individual salvation, you must understand that God's will is to save the world. Therefore, one must put forth effort for the world.

That is why throughout history, sages have always revered God. There has never been a sage who did not revere God. You must understand this. Those who have participated in the ranks of sages are the leaders of religions, and they have always taught the principles of heaven. That is, they centered on the way of heaven, humanized the heavenly feelings, and taught the principles of human morality and human emotions as the global goal to humanity. Thus, sages are not nationalists but cosmopolitans.

What is the highest sincerity among sincerities? Until now, many parents have dedicated their lives with sincerity for their children. However, there have been no individuals who have dedicated their sincerity for the nation and the world. Therefore, there must be a group that puts forth sincerity and sacrifices for the nation and the world, and what kind of group is that? It is the group that reveres religion. That is why, throughout the long course of history, while nations have perished, religions have not. Therefore, the purpose of religion will inevitably be fulfilled.

For God's will to be realized, there must be a group that puts forth sincerity for the world. God has been on the side of such groups until now. Therefore, religion must create an environment that can inevitably possess global sovereignty and dominate the world through God. If there is a central religion that puts forth sincerity for that day, in the end, the world will come under its authority. This is the phenomenon occurring in the democratic world centered around the current Christian cultural sphere. In this view, we must put forth sincerity today.

To summarize what has been said so far, it comes down to God's love and will. A person who lives with sincerity centered on that love and will lives for the individual but becomes a person who lives for the world. If there is a family that lives centered on that will and love, that family lives for the world while also living for itself. Furthermore, if there are such tribes, nations, and states, they too become tribes, nations, and states that live for the world.

Therefore, if there are thirty million people, all thirty million must uphold God's will ideologically, and if they cling to that will without falling away, this people will undoubtedly become a people that lives in accordance with that will.

Today, when we look at the Unification Church centered on God's will, if we all come together centered on that will, will you become one with God's will, even if it means losing your life? Do you love the will, have a bond of life with the will, live a process-oriented life, and can you conclude your life with the results? If you can say yes, then if God's will is true and God's love is true, you will become a true person. You must understand that such a time is coming.

God will surely test us centered on that moment. How much do I love the will? How much will I bear the cross for humanity in serving that will? How much will I be willing to sacrifice my body to love God? I must go through that testing process.

And then, I must receive the acknowledgment that it is enough.

From this perspective, today, the Republic of Korea bears the burden of a suffering national history and stands in a subjective position, enduring the tumultuous waves of the world, but I do not see this as a sorrowful thing.

If we think this way, we must consider that the difficulties of this people may actually become a blessing for us.

Those who have a strong desire to seek truth must inevitably go through negative processes to cross that boundary. Therefore, we should not feel lonely just because we are in an environment where we are not free and are in a pitiful position compared to others. Instead, we must have hope and recognize that when we step over that negative environment, there is a path to cross into a new world.

The question is whether we can become a nation that can be loyal to God when we face national trials. If the thirty million people today cannot do so, what should we do? We must stand on the path of trials, take responsibility in place of this people, and fulfill the mission of pioneers who open the way for this people. If we do so, this people will surely go that way. We must recognize that we have a significant responsibility to do this, looking at the global trends from 1970 to 1972.

Truth is not achieved in a day or two. It must go through a historical process and encompass all the eras to see the end. 

Even when looking at mountains, high mountains extend long along their ranges. They begin from a very distant place, to the point where one may not even know where they started. Whether anyone acknowledges it or not is not the issue.

You see, when you visit Jeju Island, it seems as if the entire island exists to create Hallasan. Even the flatlands are all shaped that way. Similarly, everything belonging to it must resemble that one mountain as a standard. The angles must align wherever one goes, as they belong to that mountain.

In the same way, as you head towards the standard of the peak, even if each of you is far apart, you must understand that you must have a form that can align with the peak and the angles.

Truth is not achieved all at once. Our church has walked the path of suffering until now without making excuses. We have endured every humiliation and faced opposition in various environments, yet we have no time to make excuses. Our path is busier than that. We think that the historical process is such, and we are now running up the hill towards the peak.

The period until 1972 is a historical period in which we must overcome the national grievances centered on global trends. It is the year that marks twelve years since the blessed families began, and we must carry and overcome the national grievances. Because there remains a responsibility to bear the familial cross until 1972, we must go forward.

**A Life for the Future and for the Nation and the World**  
During this period, we must prepare a historical process that aligns with all external circumstances of the world. We must recognize that this is the result shown from a principled perspective and resolve anew.

One must not respect oneself. Thinking centered on oneself can easily lead to becoming a traitor to the nation and a betrayer of the world.
is. It is also about dreaming of comfort centered around one's own family. When that becomes a betrayal to the nation and the world, or to the heavenly principles, it will be an enemy of God, an enemy of the world, and an enemy of the nation, won't it? We must not let that happen.

After all, we are pioneers who must carve out the path of goodness. Because the steps we take as such pioneers are holy, the process must also be holy, and the results must be holy as well. Even if we fall in the end, when we become a seed and a new sprout emerges from it, we must not be like a tree standing in the cracks of a mountain ridge but rather become a tree grown in fertile soil, and if we cannot bear the fruits we hoped for in our lifetime, we must live with the hope of reaping them through our descendants.

A person with such a heart who fights for future happiness is a formidable person. A group that wishes to sacrifice themselves for future victory is a fearsome group. If there is such a nation, even if it is a minority, you must understand that this nation will dominate the world in the 21st century, or the 30th century, or the 50th century.

Today, we should not be disheartened that the Republic of Korea has not achieved unification. If there are just a few people with the necessary ideology for the future and a historical tradition that can be revered by many nations, that nation will be rebuilt through those people. We must run forward with this solemn hope.

We must live with the hope of future victory rather than the victory of today. This is the life that true people can inherit. Even Jesus, when he stood at the path of his final destiny in the Garden of Gethsemane, imagined the future heaven and the world of happiness and decided to sacrifice everything for it and walk the path of death.

To the people of his time, Jesus was seen as a foolish person, and in the context of that era, he was viewed as a traitor to the nation, mocked as a madman hoping for miracles, and sadly faded away. However, the intention he held was one that no one in the world could hold, and because of that intention, he was able to move the world and establish a new cultural world.

No matter how capable you are or how hard you try, if you live for yourself, the end is near. However, if you live for the nation, the country, and the world, you must understand that the end is far away.

Until now, that has been the standard of the teacher's life. The reason the teacher has devoted his life to this belief and has come to this point today is because God has cooperated. I never think that I have achieved this because of my own abilities. It is because God has cooperated. Without a doubt, God has cooperated. It is because God has always encouraged me during difficult times and lonely paths that I have been able to remain on this path and meet you today. This will also be the case for you.

From now on, you must know how much of the path centered on the individual, family, tribe, and nation remains and walk that path. What will your appearance be like in the process of connecting that path to reach the destination? This is the question.

The motivation is tremendous and serious. You must understand that motivation is constantly moving for the sake of the overall purpose. Just as your heart works tirelessly to maintain your life even while you sleep, motivation is relentless. That is why God also has no night or day. He does not distinguish between night and day to choose when to do His work. He is in a position of motivation that cannot rest, a subjective position, and therefore continues to work.

When we think of this, we must not become ancestors criticized by our descendants in the process of inheriting what God initiated. We must not become a cowardly group that is slandered by our descendants due to our environment. If you did not know this path, that is one thing, but now that you know the great road you must walk and the direction in which you must pave that road, you must push through any difficulties that arise. Isn't that the responsibility of those who pave this path? If that path has already been paved, you must walk it correctly. That path is already paved. If you cannot walk this path, you will fail to present the direction of that already paved path.

Completion of Truth

Now, in the midst of this, as we welcome the beginning of November, we must become a group that sincerely dedicates itself to this nation and the world. We must overcome to the point where we carry the world on our backs and our bones melt away for the sake of fulfilling our responsibilities.

When a tree is grafted, the grafting involves passing through the boundary where its life elements are exhausted and receiving new sap. In the same way, whether it is a nation or an individual, we are destined to be grafted around a new ideal, and because you are in such a position, you must cross that boundary. In other words, the origin of a new beginning is sought through the process of self-denial. This has been the traditional reality woven by history until now.

We have presented the tremendous task of a victorious unification front and fought around it since the 1970s. During that time, we have held many international events such as the Asian Victory Conference, the WACL (World Anti-Communist League) held in Japan, and the 777 couple international joint wedding ceremony. There are also events this November, and we are carrying out intensified events. Through these, we must lay the foundation for all the plans of the 1970s in this year. Therefore, you must understand how great your responsibility is.

There is also the issue of raising the necessary funds to establish the World Mission Headquarters in Yeouido. It feels like trying to catch a running tiger with bare hands. From now until the end of February next year, we must raise more than 400 million won with bare hands. This is possible.

We can create history and pave a new era. What we have done until now has not been because we had a lot of money. We have pioneered even in the midst of scarcity. We must go forward with the belief that if God cooperates, we can succeed. The question is whether you, who are in a relative position centered around the teacher, will take responsibility or not. You must understand that if we unite, we can create a new world.

We must become true people, establish a true nation, and create a true world where we can serve God and receive God's true love. That is life, and you must understand this.

The history until the truth is realized is long. It is not something that is accomplished simply. If there is a nation that has endured for hundreds of years and has inherited patience, that nation can inherit thousands of years of history. Furthermore, if there is a group that endures the path of suffering for thousands of years to inherit the truth, they will inherit tens of thousands of years of history.

In this era, the question is how we will stand at the forefront of our nation through ourselves and how we will proceed in the face of the intention we desire. Will we turn back, move forward, or go sideways? There are many paths. If we turn back here, we will surely fall into a trap, and if we go sideways, we will surely be invaded by thieves. There is no other way to go. If there were another way, I would have already taken it. If there were another path, who would endure this suffering while being scorned? This is the only path; if it were not, it would be blocked along the way. It is the fate of unification.

Perhaps that is why when I look at your faces, they all seem to be born with strong fates. If you say you can't go because it's too hard, who would you pass that trivial fate onto? You must completely shed it. You must strip away the shell of fate until only the bare bones remain, and then you must reshape and carry on. Until that is all stripped away, even if you must remain and die, you must have the resolve not to change.

As mentioned earlier, you must love God centered around your intentions. When God walks with the individual, the individual must run toward God, and when He walks with the family, the family must run toward God. Also, when God holds onto the tribe, all of you in the church must fulfill your tribal mission and run toward God. If the nation is then presented before God, this becomes a global issue.

If thousands or tens of thousands of people grab your neck and pull, will your neck break, or will you rise up with the strength pulling from above? If you rise up, both the pulling strength must be strong and your neck must be sturdy. In that sense, the teacher does not owe you anything. I absolutely do not owe you. That is certain. I may do things for you, but I do not owe you. A leader who is in debt will fail. His fate will be miserable. God also absolutely hates being in debt. The more you know, the more you stand in a position where you must repay that debt. If you understand the intention, you must repay that debt. Even if we all say we are for the intention, the root is more important than the trunk, the trunk more than the branches, and the branches more than the leaves.

Truth is universal. It is not personal but universal. Moreover, truth is historical. It was needed in the past, is needed in the present, and will be needed in the future. Because truth is universal, its value must be eternal. So what does it mean to be universal? Think about it. Can a person's intention be universal? If it is the intention I am speaking of here, then if there is someone better than me, they can claim, "Is that your intention? My intention is this." The universal intention is not the intention of any saint. The intentions of Western saints and Eastern saints differ. Because their national backgrounds, cultural backgrounds, and traditional connections are different, they can make different claims. Therefore, their claims cannot become universal intentions. They can only be sectarian intentions.

Can the center of the intention we can uphold as universal be found on the earth? It cannot be found on the earth. The matters of the earth are without consciousness. People do not want to follow the intentions of those on this earth. People wish to follow the intentions of a higher absolute being. That universal intention is the intention of God, the absolute being.

That is why Jesus is considered wonderful. Jesus said, "Do not worry about what you will eat, what you will drink, or what you will wear. For the pagans run after all these things. But seek first his kingdom and his righteousness" (Matthew 6:31). What kingdom is this? Is it the kingdom of Israel? It is not the kingdom that Jesus himself desires. It is the kingdom that God desires. It is the kingdom that the absolute being, the center of truth, wishes for. Then what does that intention mean? It is the intention to establish that kingdom. You must understand this. That intention is absolute, true intention, and it is not a human intention but God's intention.

So who is God? What kind of relationship does He want to have with humanity? We call God the God of love, but what kind of position does He want to establish a loving relationship with us? Does He want to relate as friends? He wants to relate in the closest position. So what is the closest position? It is the relationship between a father and his children. There is no closer position than that. God is my Father. How wonderful is that? If we are to love, we must love from the position of a father and his children; otherwise, how can we say we have loved? If it is not from that position, it is all false love.

The most necessary and valuable love is the love that comes from this position. Because there is no relationship beyond that of father and son between God and humanity, He wishes to establish a relationship of love as a father to His children. Furthermore, humanity desires to receive parental love from God. Do you want to receive parental love from the position of an adopted child? Do you want to receive love from the position of a friend? You will want to receive love from the position of a son or a daughter or a wife. This is the essence of Christianity. The relationship of Jesus as the bridegroom and God as the Father has clarified that relationship.

Then, if that absolute God is my Father, then the will of that Father becomes my will. God's will is a universal will. That will is not just for the Republic of Korea. It is a will to save the world, and those who are faithful to that will for the sake of the world will join the ranks of saints.

To become a filial son and a loyal subject, one must have the will to love the world and serve the world; this is God's will. Therefore, knowing that loving and serving the world is the way to love God, you must live with that heart. What is the principle of a person who thinks and lives their entire life like this? It is globalism, it is cosmopolitanism. Such a person speaks only that speech, and when they work, they can only do that work. Such a person is a true person. Furthermore, a family that lives like this is a true family, and a tribe formed by such families is a true tribe. The country that lives for the world centered on this is a true country, and the world formed in this way is the true world, that is, the kingdom of heaven.

Truth is connected to the world. It is also absolute and historical. It encompasses the past, present, and future. Therefore, truth is the historical fruit, the center of this era, and the starting point toward the future, and you must understand this. That is why in the Unification Church, true parents emerge. True parents are the parents of humanity found within God's will. A true family is a family that has inherited the will of the true parents. A true tribe is also a tribe formed around the true parents. You must know this and strive to become true people. A true person loves their country, loves the world, and loves God.

Even if you die, the world must remain. God's will for the world must remain, and God's love for the world must remain. Therefore, even if you die, you must leave those things behind. A person who sacrifices their life to leave those behind becomes a filial son and a loyal subject.

We do not need a one-day filial son or a one-day loyal subject. A one-day filial son can be anyone, even the most wicked robber. A one-day loyal subject can also be anyone; they can become one as soon as they repent. God desires a person who is born as a filial son and loyal subject, lives as a filial son and loyal subject, and dies as a filial son and loyal subject. What kind of filial son would you desire? Those who are newly introduced here may not understand this.

When comparing you to the teacher, the teacher is likely more of a filial son before God than you are. This is because I have devoted my life to this work until now. However, I never think that I have fulfilled the duty of a filial son. The more I go, the more I feel my shortcomings. I have not fulfilled the duties of a filial son or loyal subject.
A person who thinks ends up as a filial son or loyal subject. A person who protests, saying, "I am a filial son, I am a loyal subject, why don't you recognize me?" is someone who retreats from that stance. As time goes on, one discovers that the way of filial piety remains, and the way of loyalty remains, and it is only those who take fulfilling that filial duty as their life philosophy who can become the heavenly filial sons and loyal subjects. You must understand this.

How many years have you truly been loyal to the cause? Are you all going to go for the cause? Will you all go? Raise your hand if you are going to go for the cause. Your hands go up easily. Put them down. How many years are you going to be loyal to the cause? "What do you mean by how many years? Just seven years is enough!" Is that what you think? And then you say, "God, bless me." Can you become a filial son like that?

You must understand that there are levels and histories in the paths of loyal subjects and filial sons. We must think broadly, deeply, and highly. If I stretch myself out in the long run, my existence disappears; if I spread myself out in the wide, I disappear; if I elevate myself to a high place, I disappear. However, that does not mean that I ultimately cease to exist. Therefore, where one lives for God's will, there is peace. 

Why does a child long for the embrace of their parents? It is because the parents live for their children, and there is peace in that.

Even if the world shakes, we cannot rest. The secret to the prosperity of the Republic of Korea is simple. The sovereign must live for the people. The rulers must live for the nation and the people. You must know that this is the path of truth, and you must walk this path. If we fail, then come to me and protest.

Throughout my life, people have said that I would fail and disappear, but I have not failed. I have nothing to envy in this world. Although I was born as a man of Korea, if I give orders here, there are people who will dance even if I say so from abroad, and they will do anything. No one in the world can follow me in this regard. Why is that? It is not because I have good means or skills to manipulate people in front and behind. It is because, without saying a word, their hearts are naturally drawn to me. When I say to do something, if they do not, they feel troubled in their hearts. You all feel the same way.

When the teacher tells you to mobilize everyone, who wants to be mobilized? In fact, I do not want to mobilize either. Pretty young ladies who like to dress up nicely and wear makeup do not want to go out and get tanned. Who would like to see a face that does not look good? I do not like to see faces that do not look good either. However, if we do not mobilize, both will fail. So, should we go the way of failure or the way of prosperity? To go the way of prosperity, we have no choice but to mobilize. It is like crying while eating mustard. It is unavoidable. Knowing this, you must not go the way of failure.

Is the phrase "始終如一" (consistent from beginning to end) a good phrase or a bad phrase? "It is a good phrase." It is a good phrase, but is it easy to do? "It is difficult." Then, is the phrase "苦盡甘來" (after hardship comes happiness) a good phrase or a bad phrase? "It is a good phrase." Is it easy or difficult to do? "It is difficult." How difficult is it? It is more difficult than dying. However, those who have prepared for death and have overcome it can taste the sweetness of having conquered death.

You already know this and have started, so you must be consistent. Even if you go to prison, even if the entire Republic of Korea opposes you and the world shakes, we cannot rest. We cannot be swayed by opposition. The Unification Church is different from the people of the world. Even if someone tries to bribe us, it does not work.

In society, to get people to work, you have to buy them cigarettes or lunch; otherwise, they will not work properly. Even in our factory, when people from society come and think we are like them, they ask for work and transactions, and when they offer money for lunch, our church members say, "What is this?" They do not act like worldly people and do not know how to greet. Bribery does not work on us. When the people of the world look at us, they see us as naive, like boiled chestnuts that they can easily take. However, if they eat the wrong one, they could end up with diarrhea or worse. (Laughter) This is our Unification Church.

Even nowadays, there are many rumors about our church. However, we will not be swayed by them. If there are rumors, it means we are doing something. We are busy with our path. Because of that, newspaper reporters say that the Unification Church does not know how to handle the media. However, we do not need to know that. We are busier with our path than to be concerned about that. Please do not get involved in such matters and focus on achieving our goals. Do you understand? "Yes."

Now, we should roll up our sleeves and run forward. In the past, even girls around ten or eleven years old went out to evangelize alone, but that is not the case anymore. Now, we will send out teams centered around middle-aged women. We will organize teams of about ten people to evangelize throughout the neighborhood. This is progress. In the future, the team of ten evangelists will grow to one hundred, and when they go to evangelize in a village, it will come to that. If that happens, those who do not believe in the Unification Church will have to either die or move somewhere else. (Laughter)

If the Korean people do not evangelize and believe, Westerners will come and do it, and Japanese people will come and do it. That will surely happen. So, if you do not want to see that happen, you must either believe in the Unification Church or flee or die. That is how things will unfold.

We may seem like nothing now, but when we unite, we can break through stone. When you light the fuse of dynamite, it may seem insignificant and like a mere spark, but when it ignites the detonator and explodes, you will see. Who is stronger, me or you? At that moment, even a mountain can be shattered. We must go out with such determination. Do you understand? "Yes."

Truth is eternal, and this meaning is what all people should pursue. Today is the first day of November! It is a pleasant day. There are about 60 days left in this year, and in 1970, we must lay the groundwork needed for the 1970s. Therefore, we are trying to purchase about ten thousand pyeong of land in Yeouido. If each person buys just one pyeong, we might have the largest land in Yeouido.

Now we must earn money diligently. Therefore, in the future, all Unification Church members should build buildings to live in. If we work hard, it is not impossible. If others work for a century, and we work day and night for a century, we can live twice as well as they do. That is why our factory is working even at night. It may be tiring, but let's give it a try. If we live well, we will save our nation and humanity. We must go forward with such a goal.

Truth is eternal, and the meaning of truth is God's will. Therefore, this is the meaning that all people should pursue. You must understand that only by living centered on this meaning and emulating God's love can truth be established, and you should take this as your life philosophy. You will not fail.

Have I failed? I started with empty hands. Even if it involves hundreds of millions of won, I can do it. If I cannot do it in Korea, I have laid the foundation to move the world. Even while being chased and persecuted, I have laid a global foundation. It is not because I have good means that this has happened, but because I understood and executed the principles correctly. If you follow these principles, you will undoubtedly not fail. Therefore, I hope you will also move according to these principles. Do you understand? "Yes."

Now, the blessed families' women must receive training at the Sutak-ri training center and go out starting from the first day of December. Do you know this? We will send out about 1,200 people, and the teacher will observe their activities. If they do not engage in activities, even if the teacher gives them a hard time, no one will protest. The teacher is already doing more than that and asking them to do it. Those who cannot do that have nothing to do with me. You must know this and go forth with vigor for this nation and this people. We must advance. Do you understand? "Yes." Raise your hand if you are willing to go that way. Put your hands down.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, before your high and precious will, we are descendants burdened with historical debts, and we must repay this debt. We must take on the responsibility of the priests who must indemnify the sins of the times, even if it leaves bloodstains on our white garments. We earnestly ask that you be with your children who understand this with your boundless mercy and love. And allow us to be unchanging sons and daughters before the hope of tomorrow.

We must become true people. We must become true families. We must become a true church and a true nation. We must establish a true world. Please allow these to be made clear to them.

On this earth, everything is surrounded by an evil environment that opposes truth. In such an environment, we earnestly hope that your children can reveal their pure and powerful selves with the passion of truth without change, Father.

From now on, let every plan be for your exaltation and for your glory to shine, and let this be a time when we pledge to fulfill the duties of filial piety and loyalty before you, ready to fight and sacrifice. May your protection be with such children forever.

We earnestly ask that you embrace and protect the many children scattered throughout South Korea and the world with your wide and deep love, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
